<p>The conditions are derived from the requirements:</p>
<ol>
<li><p><strong>Is the first name entered?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Is the last name entered?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Is the email entered and valid?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Is the phone number entered?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Is the appointment date/time entered?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Is the appointment date/time available?</strong> (Yes/No)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<h3 id="heading-identify-the-outcomes" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-identify-the-outcomes" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-identify-the-outcomes" style="height: 36px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Identify the outcomes</h3>
<p>The possible actions based on the conditions are:</p>
<ol>
<li><p>Display "All fields are required."</p>
</li>
<li><p>Display "Please enter a valid email."</p>
</li>
<li><p>Display "Appointment not available. Please choose another."</p>
</li>
<li><p>Schedule the appointment successfully.</p>
</li>
</ol>

<h3 id="heading-explanation-of-scenarios" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-explanation-of-scenarios" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-explanation-of-scenarios" style="height: 36px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Explanation of scenarios</h3>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>C1–C6:</strong> One or more fields are missing. The system should display "All fields are required."</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>C7–C8:</strong> All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display "Appointment not available."</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>C9:</strong> All fields are entered correctly, and the appointment is available. The system should schedule the appointment successfully.</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>C10:</strong> All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display "Appointment not available."</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>C11–C12:</strong> All fields are correct, but the email is invalid. The system should display "Please enter a valid email."</p>
</li>
<li><p><strong>C13–C16:</strong> Various valid/invalid combinations where the email or availability determines the outcome.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Q2)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><h3 id="heading-scenario-1-testing-access-based-on-user-roles" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-1-testing-access-based-on-user-roles" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-1-testing-access-based-on-user-roles" style="height: 36px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a><strong>Scenario 1: Testing Access Based on User Roles</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Objective:</strong> Ensure the app enforces correct access permissions for basic, premium, and admin users.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-test-steps" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Test Steps:</h4>
<ol>
<li><p><strong>Basic User Access:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Log in as a basic user.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt to access limited features (e.g., view-only sections, restricted tools).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt to access premium features and advanced settings.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Premium User Access:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Log in as a premium user.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt to access all features of the app.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt to access advanced settings reserved for admin users.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Admin User Access:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Log in as an admin user.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt to access all features, including advanced settings.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Attempt actions like managing other users, viewing logs, or updating configurations.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Test for unauthorized actions:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>As each user type, try performing an action that is not authorized (e.g., basic user trying to access premium content).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 id="heading-expected-results" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Expected Results:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>Basic users can only access limited features and are denied access to premium features and advanced settings with an appropriate error message like: <strong>"You do not have access to this feature. Upgrade your account to unlock more features."</strong></p>
</li>
<li><p>Premium users can access all features except admin-level settings. Unauthorized actions should display a clear error message: <strong>"This action is restricted to admin users."</strong></p>
</li>
<li><p>Admin users can access all features and perform all actions.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-additional-considerations" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Additional Considerations:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>Ensure error messages are consistent and user-friendly.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Verify that unauthorized attempts do not cause the app to crash.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3 id="heading-scenario-2-testing-account-creation-deletion-and-password-standards" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-2-testing-account-creation-deletion-and-password-standards" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-2-testing-account-creation-deletion-and-password-standards" style="height: 36px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a><strong>Scenario 2: Testing Account Creation, Deletion, and Password Standards</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Objective:</strong> Ensure users can successfully create and delete accounts, passwords meet complexity standards, and confirmation emails are sent upon successful account creation.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-test-steps-1" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps-1" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps-1" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Test Steps:</h4>
<ol>
<li><p><strong>Account Creation:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Attempt to create an account with:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>A valid email and password that meets the complexity standards (e.g., minimum 8 characters, mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, special characters).</p>
</li>
<li><p>A weak password (e.g., "12345") and check for rejection with an appropriate error message.</p>
</li>
<li><p>A missing or invalid email (e.g., "user@com") and check for rejection.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p>Verify that a confirmation email is sent upon successful account creation.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Account Deletion:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Log in with an existing account.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Navigate to the account settings and delete the account.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Verify that the account is deleted successfully and that the user can no longer log in with the same credentials.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Password Standards:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Test password validation rules, including:</p>
<ul>
<li><p>Minimum/maximum length requirements.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Presence of special characters, numbers, and uppercase/lowercase letters.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 id="heading-expected-results-1" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results-1" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results-1" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Expected Results:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>Account creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent with a message like: <strong>"Your account has been successfully created. Please check your email to confirm your registration."</strong></p>
</li>
<li><p>Account creation fails for invalid inputs with clear error messages (e.g., <strong>"Password must include at least 8 characters, a number, and a special character."</strong>).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Account deletion removes the user data and prevents further login.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Password validation works as per the standards, and invalid passwords are rejected with appropriate messages.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-additional-considerations-1" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations-1" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations-1" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Additional Considerations:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>Check the email's spam folder to ensure confirmation emails aren't flagged as spam.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Verify that accounts are not created or deleted twice due to race conditions or errors.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3 id="heading-scenario-3-testing-app-navigation-and-performance" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-3-testing-app-navigation-and-performance" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-scenario-3-testing-app-navigation-and-performance" style="height: 36px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a><strong>Scenario 3: Testing App Navigation and Performance</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Objective:</strong> Ensure seamless navigation, no crashes, and appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-test-steps-2" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps-2" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-test-steps-2" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Test Steps:</h4>
<ol>
<li><p><strong>App Navigation:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Log in as a user (basic, premium, or admin).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Navigate through all app features and settings.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Check for responsiveness, load times, and any UI/UX glitches.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Performance Testing:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Stress-test the app by navigating quickly, performing multiple actions simultaneously, or opening multiple instances.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Test on different devices and operating systems to check compatibility.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><p><strong>Error Messages:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Attempt unauthorized actions (e.g., basic user accessing premium content).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Disconnect the internet and try performing an action to check offline behavior.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Input invalid data in forms and observe error handling.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h4 id="heading-expected-results-2" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results-2" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-expected-results-2" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Expected Results:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>App navigation is smooth, with no crashes or performance degradation.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Pages load quickly, and the UI is responsive across devices.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Unauthorized actions display clear error messages (e.g., <strong>"Feature unavailable for your account type."</strong>).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Offline actions show appropriate warnings or suggestions (e.g., <strong>"You are offline. Please reconnect to continue."</strong>).</p>
</li>
<li><p>Invalid inputs are flagged immediately with detailed error messages.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="heading-additional-considerations-2" class="permalink-heading"><a class="permalink-heading-button" title="Permalink" href="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations-2" data-clipboard-text="https://testcase-design.hashnode.dev/testcasedesign#heading-additional-considerations-2" style="height: 28px;"><span class="hidden">Permalink</span><svg class="h-4 w-4 fill-current dark:text-white" viewBox="0 0 512 512"><path d="M301.148 394.702l-79.2 79.19c-50.778 50.799-133.037 50.824-183.84 0-50.799-50.778-50.824-133.037 0-183.84l79.19-79.2a132.833 132.833 0 013.532-3.403c7.55-7.005 19.795-2.004 20.208 8.286.193 4.807.598 9.607 1.216 14.384.481 3.717-.746 7.447-3.397 10.096-16.48 16.469-75.142 75.128-75.3 75.286-36.738 36.759-36.731 96.188 0 132.94 36.759 36.738 96.188 36.731 132.94 0l79.2-79.2.36-.36c36.301-36.672 36.14-96.07-.37-132.58-8.214-8.214-17.577-14.58-27.585-19.109-4.566-2.066-7.426-6.667-7.134-11.67a62.197 62.197 0 012.826-15.259c2.103-6.601 9.531-9.961 15.919-7.28 15.073 6.324 29.187 15.62 41.435 27.868 50.688 50.689 50.679 133.17 0 183.851zm-90.296-93.554c12.248 12.248 26.362 21.544 41.435 27.868 6.388 2.68 13.816-.68 15.919-7.28a62.197 62.197 0 002.826-15.259c.292-5.003-2.569-9.604-7.134-11.67-10.008-4.528-19.371-10.894-27.585-19.109-36.51-36.51-36.671-95.908-.37-132.58l.36-.36 79.2-79.2c36.752-36.731 96.181-36.738 132.94 0 36.731 36.752 36.738 96.181 0 132.94-.157.157-58.819 58.817-75.3 75.286-2.651 2.65-3.878 6.379-3.397 10.096a163.156 163.156 0 011.216 14.384c.413 10.291 12.659 15.291 20.208 8.286a131.324 131.324 0 003.532-3.403l79.19-79.2c50.824-50.803 50.799-133.062 0-183.84-50.802-50.824-133.062-50.799-183.84 0l-79.2 79.19c-50.679 50.682-50.688 133.163 0 183.851z"></path></svg></a>Additional Considerations:</h4>
<ul>
<li><p>Test app navigation in both portrait and landscape modes.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Use a performance monitoring tool to track memory usage and load times.</p>
</li>
<li><p>Log and report crashes with detailed steps to reproduce.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>

              var SUPPORTS_PASSIVE = false;
              try {
                var opts = Object.defineProperty({}, 'passive', {
                  get: function() {
                    SUPPORTS_PASSIVE = true;
                  }
                });
                window.addEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);
                window.removeEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);
              } catch (e) {}
            </script><script type="text/javascript">
              // Array.prototype.flat polyfill
              if (!Array.prototype.flat) {
                // eslint-disable-next-line no-extend-native
                Object.defineProperty(Array.prototype, 'flat', {
                  configurable: true,
                  writable: true,
                  value() {
                    // eslint-disable-next-line prefer-rest-params
                    const depth = typeof arguments[0] === 'undefined' ? 1 : Number(arguments[0]) || 0;
                    const result = [];
                    const { forEach } = result;

                    // eslint-disable-next-line no-var
                    var flatDeep = function (arr, depth) {
                      forEach.call(arr, (val) => {
                        if (depth > 0 && Array.isArray(val)) {
                          flatDeep(val, depth - 1);
                        } else {
                          result.push(val);
                        }
                      });
                    };

                    flatDeep(this, depth);
                    return result;
                  },
                });
              }

**Q1)**\\n\\nThe conditions are derived from the requirements:\\n\\n1. **Is the first name entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n2. **Is the last name entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n3. **Is the email entered and valid?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n4. **Is the phone number entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n5. **Is the appointment date/time entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n6. **Is the appointment date/time available?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n\\n---\\n\\n### Identify the outcomes\\n\\nThe possible actions based on the conditions are:\\n\\n1. Display \\\"All fields are required.\\\"\\n    \\n2. Display \\\"Please enter a valid email.\\\"\\n    \\n3. Display \\\"Appointment not available. Please choose another.\\\"\\n    \\n4. Schedule the appointment successfully.\\n    \\n\\n**Decision table** by listing all possible conditions and the resulting actions.\\n\\n| Condition/Scenario | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | C6 | C7 | C8 | C9 | C10 | C11 | C12 | C13 | C14 | C15 | C16 |\\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\\n| First Name Entered? | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Last Name Entered? | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Email Entered and Valid? | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Phone Number Entered? | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Appointment Date/Time Entered? | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Appointment Date/Time Available? | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | No | No | Yes | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| **Action: All Fields Required** | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No |\\n| **Action: Invalid Email** | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | No | No | No | No |\\n| **Action: Appointment Not Available** | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | Yes | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | No |\\n| **Action: Schedule Appointment** | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | No | No | Yes | Yes |\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Explanation of scenarios\\n\\n* **C1–C6:** One or more fields are missing. The system should display \\\"All fields are required.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C7–C8:** All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display \\\"Appointment not available.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C9:** All fields are entered correctly, and the appointment is available. The system should schedule the appointment successfully.\\n    \\n* **C10:** All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display \\\"Appointment not available.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C11–C12:** All fields are correct, but the email is invalid. The system should display \\\"Please enter a valid email.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C13–C16:** Various valid/invalid combinations where the email or availability determines the outcome.\\n    \\n\\n**Q2)**\\n\\n* ### **Scenario 1: Testing Access Based on User Roles**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure the app enforces correct access permissions for basic, premium, and admin users.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **Basic User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a basic user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access limited features (e.g., view-only sections, restricted tools).\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access premium features and advanced settings.\\n            \\n    2. **Premium User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a premium user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access all features of the app.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access advanced settings reserved for admin users.\\n            \\n    3. **Admin User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as an admin user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access all features, including advanced settings.\\n            \\n        * Attempt actions like managing other users, viewing logs, or updating configurations.\\n            \\n    4. **Test for unauthorized actions:**\\n        \\n        * As each user type, try performing an action that is not authorized (e.g., basic user trying to access premium content).\\n            \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * Basic users can only access limited features and are denied access to premium features and advanced settings with an appropriate error message like: **\\\"You do not have access to this feature. Upgrade your account to unlock more features.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Premium users can access all features except admin-level settings. Unauthorized actions should display a clear error message: **\\\"This action is restricted to admin users.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Admin users can access all features and perform all actions.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Ensure error messages are consistent and user-friendly.\\n        \\n    * Verify that unauthorized attempts do not cause the app to crash.\\n        \\n    \\n    ---\\n    \\n    ### **Scenario 2: Testing Account Creation, Deletion, and Password Standards**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure users can successfully create and delete accounts, passwords meet complexity standards, and confirmation emails are sent upon successful account creation.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **Account Creation:**\\n        \\n        * Attempt to create an account with:\\n            \\n            * A valid email and password that meets the complexity standards (e.g., minimum 8 characters, mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, special characters).\\n                \\n            * A weak password (e.g., \\\"12345\\\") and check for rejection with an appropriate error message.\\n                \\n            * A missing or invalid email (e.g., \\\"user@com\\\") and check for rejection.\\n                \\n        * Verify that a confirmation email is sent upon successful account creation.\\n            \\n    2. **Account Deletion:**\\n        \\n        * Log in with an existing account.\\n            \\n        * Navigate to the account settings and delete the account.\\n            \\n        * Verify that the account is deleted successfully and that the user can no longer log in with the same credentials.\\n            \\n    3. **Password Standards:**\\n        \\n        * Test password validation rules, including:\\n            \\n            * Minimum/maximum length requirements.\\n                \\n            * Presence of special characters, numbers, and uppercase/lowercase letters.\\n                \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * Account creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent with a message like: **\\\"Your account has been successfully created. Please check your email to confirm your registration.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Account creation fails for invalid inputs with clear error messages (e.g., **\\\"Password must include at least 8 characters, a number, and a special character.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Account deletion removes the user data and prevents further login.\\n        \\n    * Password validation works as per the standards, and invalid passwords are rejected with appropriate messages.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Check the email's spam folder to ensure confirmation emails aren't flagged as spam.\\n        \\n    * Verify that accounts are not created or deleted twice due to race conditions or errors.\\n        \\n    \\n    ---\\n    \\n    ### **Scenario 3: Testing App Navigation and Performance**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure seamless navigation, no crashes, and appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **App Navigation:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a user (basic, premium, or admin).\\n            \\n        * Navigate through all app features and settings.\\n            \\n        * Check for responsiveness, load times, and any UI/UX glitches.\\n            \\n    2. **Performance Testing:**\\n        \\n        * Stress-test the app by navigating quickly, performing multiple actions simultaneously, or opening multiple instances.\\n            \\n        * Test on different devices and operating systems to check compatibility.\\n            \\n    3. **Error Messages:**\\n        \\n        * Attempt unauthorized actions (e.g., basic user accessing premium content).\\n            \\n        * Disconnect the internet and try performing an action to check offline behavior.\\n            \\n        * Input invalid data in forms and observe error handling.\\n            \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * App navigation is smooth, with no crashes or performance degradation.\\n        \\n    * Pages load quickly, and the UI is responsive across devices.\\n        \\n    * Unauthorized actions display clear error messages (e.g., **\\\"Feature unavailable for your account type.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Offline actions show appropriate warnings or suggestions (e.g., **\\\"You are offline. Please reconnect to continue.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Invalid inputs are flagged immediately with detailed error messages.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Test app navigation in both portrait and landscape modes.\\n        \\n    * Use a performance monitoring tool to track memory usage and load times.\\n        \\n    * Log and report crashes with detailed steps to reproduce.\\n        \\n    \\n    ---\",\"content\":\"\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-q1\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eQ1)\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cp\u003eThe conditions are derived from the requirements:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the first name entered?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the last name entered?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the email entered and valid?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the phone number entered?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the appointment date/time entered?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIs the appointment date/time available?\u003c/strong\u003e (Yes/No)\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-identify-the-outcomes\\\"\u003eIdentify the outcomes\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cp\u003eThe possible actions based on the conditions are:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eDisplay \\\"All fields are required.\\\"\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eDisplay \\\"Please enter a valid email.\\\"\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eDisplay \\\"Appointment not available. id=\\\"heading-scenario-1-testing-access-based-on-user-roles\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 1: Testing Access Based on User Roles\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure the app enforces correct access permissions for basic, premium, and admin users.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBasic User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a basic user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access limited features (e.g., view-only sections, restricted tools).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access premium features and advanced settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePremium User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a premium user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access all features of the app.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access advanced settings reserved for admin users.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdmin User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as an admin user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access all features, including advanced settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt actions like managing other users, viewing logs, or updating configurations.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTest for unauthorized actions:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003eAs each user type, try performing an action that is not authorized (e.g., basic user trying to access premium content).\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eBasic users can only access limited features and are denied access to premium features and advanced settings with an appropriate error message like: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"You do not have access to this feature. Upgrade your account to unlock more features.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePremium users can access all features except admin-level settings. Unauthorized actions should display a clear error message: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"This action is restricted to admin users.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAdmin users can access all features and perform all actions.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eEnsure error messages are consistent and user-friendly.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that unauthorized attempts do not cause the app to crash.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-scenario-2-testing-account-creation-deletion-and-password-standards\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 2: Testing Account Creation, Deletion, and Password Standards\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure users can successfully create and delete accounts, passwords meet complexity standards, and confirmation emails are sent upon successful account creation.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps-1\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccount Creation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to create an account with:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA valid email and password that meets the complexity standards (e.g., minimum 8 characters, mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, special characters).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA weak password (e.g., \\\"12345\\\") and check for rejection with an appropriate error message.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA missing or invalid email (e.g., \\\"user@com\\\") and check for rejection.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that a confirmation email is sent upon successful account creation.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccount Deletion:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in with an existing account.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eNavigate to the account settings and delete the account.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that the account is deleted successfully and that the user can no longer log in with the same credentials.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePassword Standards:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest password validation rules, including:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eMinimum/maximum length requirements.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePresence of special characters, numbers, and uppercase/lowercase letters.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results-1\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent with a message like: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Your account has been successfully created. Please check your email to confirm your registration.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount creation fails for invalid inputs with clear error messages (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Password must include at least 8 characters, a number, and a special character.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount deletion removes the user data and prevents further login.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePassword validation works as per the standards, and invalid passwords are rejected with appropriate messages.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations-1\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eCheck the email's spam folder to ensure confirmation emails aren't flagged as spam.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that accounts are not created or deleted twice due to race conditions or errors.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-scenario-3-testing-app-navigation-and-performance\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 3: Testing App Navigation and Performance\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure seamless navigation, no crashes, and appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps-2\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApp Navigation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a user (basic, premium, or admin).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eNavigate through all app features and settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eCheck for responsiveness, load times, and any UI/UX glitches.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePerformance Testing:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eStress-test the app by navigating quickly, performing multiple actions simultaneously, or opening multiple instances.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest on different devices and operating systems to check compatibility.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eError Messages:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt unauthorized actions (e.g., basic user accessing premium content).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eDisconnect the internet and try performing an action to check offline behavior.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eInput invalid data in forms and observe error handling.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results-2\\\"\u003eExpected numbers, special characters).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA weak password (e.g., \\\"12345\\\") and check for rejection with an appropriate error id=\\\"heading-expected-results-1\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps-2\\\"\u003eTest devices.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eUnauthorized actions display clear error messages (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Feature unavailable for your account type.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eOffline actions show appropriate warnings or suggestions (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"You are offline. Please reconnect to continue.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eInvalid inputs are flagged immediately with detailed error messages.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations-2\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest app navigation in both portrait and landscape modes.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eUse a performance monitoring tool to track memory usage and load times.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog and report crashes with detailed steps to reproduce.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\",\"markdown\":\"### **Q1)**\\n\\nThe conditions are derived from the requirements:\\n\\n1. **Is the first name entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n2. **Is the last name entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n3. **Is the email entered and valid?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n4. **Is the phone number entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n5. **Is the appointment date/time entered?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n6. **Is the appointment date/time available?** (Yes/No)\\n    \\n\\n---\\n\\n### Identify the outcomes\\n\\nThe possible actions based on the conditions are:\\n\\n1. Display \\\"All fields are required.\\\"\\n    \\n2. Display \\\"Please enter a valid email.\\\"\\n    \\n3. Display \\\"Appointment not available. Please choose another.\\\"\\n    \\n4. Schedule the appointment successfully.\\n    \\n\\n**Decision table** by listing all possible conditions and the resulting actions.\\n\\n| Condition/Scenario | C1 | C2 | C3 | C4 | C5 | C6 | C7 | C8 | C9 | C10 | C11 | C12 | C13 | C14 | C15 | C16 |\\n| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |\\n| First Name Entered? | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Last Name Entered? | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Email Entered and Valid? | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Phone Number Entered? | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Appointment Date/Time Entered? | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| Appointment Date/Time Available? | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | N/A | No | No | Yes | No | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |\\n| **Action: All Fields Required** | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No |\\n| **Action: Invalid Email** | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | No | No | No | No |\\n| **Action: Appointment Not Available** | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | Yes | No | No | Yes | Yes | No | No |\\n| **Action: Schedule Appointment** | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | No | No | Yes | Yes |\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Explanation of scenarios\\n\\n* **C1–C6:** One or more fields are missing. The system should display \\\"All fields are required.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C7–C8:** All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display \\\"Appointment not available.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C9:** All fields are entered correctly, and the appointment is available. The system should schedule the appointment successfully.\\n    \\n* **C10:** All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display \\\"Appointment not available.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C11–C12:** All fields are correct, but the email is invalid. The system should display \\\"Please enter a valid email.\\\"\\n    \\n* **C13–C16:** Various valid/invalid combinations where the email or availability determines the outcome.\\n    \\n\\n**Q2)**\\n\\n* ### **Scenario 1: Testing Access Based on User Roles**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure the app enforces correct access permissions for basic, premium, and admin users.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **Basic User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a basic user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access limited features (e.g., view-only sections, restricted tools).\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access premium features and advanced settings.\\n            \\n    2. **Premium User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a premium user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access all features of the app.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access advanced settings reserved for admin users.\\n            \\n    3. **Admin User Access:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as an admin user.\\n            \\n        * Attempt to access all features, including advanced settings.\\n            \\n        * Attempt actions like managing other users, viewing logs, or updating configurations.\\n            \\n    4. **Test for unauthorized actions:**\\n        \\n        * As each user type, try performing an action that is not authorized (e.g., basic user trying to access premium content).\\n            \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * Basic users can only access limited features and are denied access to premium features and advanced settings with an appropriate error message like: **\\\"You do not have access to this feature. Upgrade your account to unlock more features.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Premium users can access all features except admin-level settings. Unauthorized actions should display a clear error message: **\\\"This action is restricted to admin users.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Admin users can access all features and perform all actions.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Ensure error messages are consistent and user-friendly.\\n        \\n    * Verify that unauthorized attempts do not cause the app to crash.\\n        \\n    \\n    ---\\n    \\n    ### **Scenario 2: Testing Account Creation, Deletion, and Password Standards**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure users can successfully create and delete accounts, passwords meet complexity standards, and confirmation emails are sent upon successful account creation.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **Account Creation:**\\n        \\n        * Attempt to create an account with:\\n            \\n            * A valid email and password that meets the complexity standards (e.g., minimum 8 characters, mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, special characters).\\n                \\n            * A weak password (e.g., \\\"12345\\\") and check for rejection with an appropriate error message.\\n                \\n            * A missing or invalid email (e.g., \\\"user@com\\\") and check for rejection.\\n                \\n        * Verify that a confirmation email is sent upon successful account creation.\\n            \\n    2. **Account Deletion:**\\n        \\n        * Log in with an existing account.\\n            \\n        * Navigate to the account settings and delete the account.\\n            \\n        * Verify that the account is deleted successfully and that the user can no longer log in with the same credentials.\\n            \\n    3. **Password Standards:**\\n        \\n        * Test password validation rules, including:\\n            \\n            * Minimum/maximum length requirements.\\n                \\n            * Presence of special characters, numbers, and uppercase/lowercase letters.\\n                \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * Account creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent with a message like: **\\\"Your account has been successfully created. Please check your email to confirm your registration.\\\"**\\n        \\n    * Account creation fails for invalid inputs with clear error messages (e.g., **\\\"Password must include at least 8 characters, a number, and a special character.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Account deletion removes the user data and prevents further login.\\n        \\n    * Password validation works as per the standards, and invalid passwords are rejected with appropriate messages.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Check the email's spam folder to ensure confirmation emails aren't flagged as spam.\\n        \\n    * Verify that accounts are not created or deleted twice due to race conditions or errors.\\n        \\n    \\n    ---\\n    \\n    ### **Scenario 3: Testing App Navigation and Performance**\\n    \\n    * **Objective:** Ensure seamless navigation, no crashes, and appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Test Steps:\\n    \\n    1. **App Navigation:**\\n        \\n        * Log in as a user (basic, premium, or admin).\\n            \\n        * Navigate through all app features and settings.\\n            \\n        * Check for responsiveness, load times, and any UI/UX glitches.\\n            \\n    2. **Performance Testing:**\\n        \\n        * Stress-test the app by navigating quickly, performing multiple actions simultaneously, or opening multiple instances.\\n            \\n        * Test on different devices and operating systems to check compatibility.\\n            \\n    3. **Error Messages:**\\n        \\n        * Attempt unauthorized actions (e.g., basic user accessing premium content).\\n            \\n        * Disconnect the internet and try performing an action to check offline behavior.\\n            \\n        * Input invalid data in forms and observe error handling.\\n            \\n    \\n    #### Expected Results:\\n    \\n    * App navigation is smooth, with no crashes or performance degradation.\\n        \\n    * Pages load quickly, and the UI is responsive across devices.\\n        \\n    * Unauthorized actions display clear error messages (e.g., **\\\"Feature unavailable for your account type.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Offline actions show appropriate warnings or suggestions (e.g., **\\\"You are offline. Please reconnect to continue.\\\"**).\\n        \\n    * Invalid inputs are flagged immediately with detailed error messages.\\n        \\n    \\n    #### Additional Considerations:\\n    \\n    * Test app navigation in both portrait and landscape modes.\\n        \\n    * Use a performance monitoring tool to track memory usage and load times.\\n        \\n    * Log and report crashes with detailed steps to reproduce.\\n        \\n    \\n id=\\\"heading-scenario-1-testing-access-based-on-user-roles\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 1: Testing Access Based on User Roles\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure the app enforces correct access permissions for basic, premium, and admin users.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBasic User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a basic user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access limited features (e.g., view-only sections, restricted tools).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access premium features and advanced settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePremium User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a premium user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access all features of the app.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access advanced settings reserved for admin users.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdmin User Access:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as an admin user.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to access all features, including advanced settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt actions like managing other users, viewing logs, or updating configurations.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTest for unauthorized actions:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003eAs each user type, try performing an action that is not authorized (e.g., basic user trying to access premium content).\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eBasic users can only access limited features and are denied access to premium features and advanced settings with an appropriate error message like: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"You do not have access to this feature. Upgrade your account to unlock more features.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePremium users can access all features except admin-level settings. Unauthorized actions should display a clear error message: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"This action is restricted to admin users.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAdmin users can access all features and perform all actions.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eEnsure error messages are consistent and user-friendly.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that unauthorized attempts do not cause the app to crash.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-scenario-2-testing-account-creation-deletion-and-password-standards\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 2: Testing Account Creation, Deletion, and Password Standards\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure users can successfully create and delete accounts, passwords meet complexity standards, and confirmation emails are sent upon successful account creation.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps-1\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccount Creation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt to create an account with:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA valid email and password that meets the complexity standards (e.g., minimum 8 characters, mix of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, special characters).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA weak password (e.g., \\\"12345\\\") and check for rejection with an appropriate error message.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eA missing or invalid email (e.g., \\\"user@com\\\") and check for rejection.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that a confirmation email is sent upon successful account creation.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccount Deletion:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in with an existing account.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eNavigate to the account settings and delete the account.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that the account is deleted successfully and that the user can no longer log in with the same credentials.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePassword Standards:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest password validation rules, including:\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eMinimum/maximum length requirements.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePresence of special characters, numbers, and uppercase/lowercase letters.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results-1\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount creation succeeds with valid inputs and a confirmation email is sent with a message like: \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Your account has been successfully created. Please check your email to confirm your registration.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount creation fails for invalid inputs with clear error messages (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Password must include at least 8 characters, a number, and a special character.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAccount deletion removes the user data and prevents further login.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePassword validation works as per the standards, and invalid passwords are rejected with appropriate messages.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations-1\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eCheck the email's spam folder to ensure confirmation emails aren't flagged as spam.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eVerify that accounts are not created or deleted twice due to race conditions or errors.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\u003ch3 id=\\\"heading-scenario-3-testing-app-navigation-and-performance\\\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScenario 3: Testing App Navigation and Performance\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/h3\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObjective:\u003c/strong\u003e Ensure seamless navigation, no crashes, and appropriate error handling for unauthorized actions.\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-test-steps-2\\\"\u003eTest Steps:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003col\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApp Navigation:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog in as a user (basic, premium, or admin).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eNavigate through all app features and settings.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eCheck for responsiveness, load times, and any UI/UX glitches.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePerformance Testing:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eStress-test the app by navigating quickly, performing multiple actions simultaneously, or opening multiple instances.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest on different devices and operating systems to check compatibility.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eError Messages:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eAttempt unauthorized actions (e.g., basic user accessing premium content).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eDisconnect the internet and try performing an action to check offline behavior.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eInput invalid data in forms and observe error handling.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ol\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-expected-results-2\\\"\u003eExpected Results:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eApp navigation is smooth, with no crashes or performance degradation.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003ePages load quickly, and the UI is responsive across devices.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eUnauthorized actions display clear error messages (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"Feature unavailable for your account type.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eOffline actions show appropriate warnings or suggestions (e.g., \u003cstrong\u003e\\\"You are offline. Please reconnect to continue.\\\"\u003c/strong\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eInvalid inputs are flagged immediately with detailed error messages.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003ch4 id=\\\"heading-additional-considerations-2\\\"\u003eAdditional Considerations:\u003c/h4\u003e\\n\u003cul\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eTest app navigation in both portrait and landscape modes.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eUse a performance monitoring tool to track memory usage and load times.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003eLog and report crashes with detailed steps to reproduce.\u003c/p\u003e\\n\u003c/li\u003e\\n\u003c/ul\u003e\\n\u003chr /\u003e\\n\",\"cuid\":\"cm4nr63kr000209jo5wfrgolr\",\"views\":4,\"title\":\"TestCaseDesign\",\"slug\":\"testcasedesign\",\"dateAdded\":\"2024-12-14T05:44:55.707Z\",\"dateUpdated\":\"2024-12-20T12:00:02.671Z\",\"type\":\"story\",\"isCoverImagePortrait\":false,\"brief\":\"Q1)\\nThe conditions are derived from the requirements:\\n\\nIs the first name entered? more fields are missing. The system should display \"All fields are required.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eC7–C8:\u003c/strong\u003e All fields are entered, but the appointment date/time is unavailable. The system should display \"Appointment not available.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eC9:\u003c/strong\u003e All fields are entered correctly, and the appointment is available.
